DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd">\n<html><head><meta name="qrichtext" content="1" /><style type="text/css">\np, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }\n</style></head><body style=" font-family:'MS Shell Dlg 2'; font-size:12pt; font-weight:72; font-style:normal;">\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Copy &amp; Paste timing and motion blocks from a KeyValues file into the text box below. Refer to the example data to the right for the general format of the data.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">The currently selected animation range is used to define the start and end frames which are adjusted and referred to by the cycle times defined below. The selected range can be modified by changing &quot;Frame Start&quot; and &quot;Frame End&quot; below.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Supported keys are listed below.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">Playback rate is a single value which will cause the selected animation to run at the specified speed. Values less than 1 will cause the animation to run slower, values greater than one will cause the animation to run faster. e.g. A value of 2 will cause the animation to run twice as fast.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">SetPlaybackRate</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">SetPlaybackRate is a series of blocks that contain two values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">Cycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">PlaybackRate</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. The cycle values for each block must not be duplicated and must be specified in order. These blocks modify the playback rate for the specific portion of the animation controlled by cycle. Cycle values are in the range of [0, 1] where 0 is the first frame of the animation and 1 is the last frame of animation.</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:10pt; font-weight:600;">OverrideMotion</span></p>\n<p style=" margin-top:12px; margin-bottom:12px; margin-left:0px; margin-right:0px; -qt-block-indent:0; text-indent:0px;"><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">OverrideMotion is a series of blocks that contain three supported values; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">StartCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">, </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">EndCycle</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> &amp; </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600;">MotionScale</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;">. </span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:600; color:#aa0000;">Movement</span><span style=" font-size:8pt; font-weight:400;"> parameters are ignored. OverrideMotion with a MotionScale value will scale the selectedtranslation values by the MotionScale value in the range of animation specified.</span></p></body></html
DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0//EN" "http://www.w3.org/TR/REC-html40/strict.dtd">\n<html><head><meta name="qrichtext" content="1" /><style type="text/css">\np, li { white-space: pre-wrap; }\n</style></head><body style=" font-family:'MS Shell Dlg 2';
